Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	Then take one thread and tie it around the shaft of the stick so that it cannot come back into the bladder; then insert the iron branch into the shaft gently, until it reaches the stone; and twist the iron branch with your hand in the stone little by little, until you can pierce the stone from the other side; if urine comes immediately, then press your hand on what is left of the stone that is inside the stick. If it breaks immediately, and with the urine, and the patient feels well;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie .i. fil desoz la piere et .i. autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les .ij. liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, tie one thread around the stone and another above it, then place the shaft in between the two threads where the stone is, then push forcefully, and remove the threads, and clean off the congealed blood from the wound; and treat until it heals.
de la piere des femmes	From the stone of women
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por .iij. choses: l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	It happens that stones are found in women's bodies, and if they occur once, it requires special care, and is forbidden for three reasons: one is that perhaps the woman is a virgin; and the second is that one cannot find a woman who knows how to reveal herself through tears, even when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a.	And the third way is that perhaps one cannot find a woman well versed in this art of surgery; and the fourth way is that the stone in a woman's body is more forward than a man's stone, for which reason it requires a deeper incision, and great fear there is.
Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier .i. caste mire subtil; et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	And if necessity requires this, you must seek out a competent midwife, and on her knowledge lead the way. If she does not find such, rather than one wise woman; and present someone well versed in women's life, or a woman who knows part of the art, and instructs them to do what you command about investigating the stone;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge: adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere; et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	And look very carefully to see if the woman is a virgin: then she should thrust her womb or base and seek for the stone; and if she finds it, force her against its base, and advise that she thrusts her womb or into the sickness, and presses her left hand on the bladder in shape.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse; puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie; et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	If she finds it, it is necessary that she move it from side to side as she enters the bladder until underneath, as long as she comes to the root of the thigh; then press against the stone at the root of the thigh against the middle of the penis, where it becomes a little swollen, and feel the stone in this part; and do not move her womb above the stone or under it, and be careful with your first small action.
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont: c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains. si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	Then press the root in the waist, if you feel the stone increase the wound until the stone can emerge forcefuly, and know that many kinds of stones are: that is to say, small and large and rough and smooth, long and round, and which have grooves. And understand their appearances to know the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	And if you do not find it, place sulfur on the point and hold for an hour until the sulfur is burned through; then return to your task, while the stone remains hard, and prepare with the instruments I instructed you about in the removal of stones within you to assist you in your work.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide; puis cure la plaie.	And if you do not find it, and it is that an artery has been cut, apply the powder to the point and hold firm with threads and needles, and do not start again, but leave the stone undisturbed so as not to accidentally kill the patient; then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has subsided and the limb is restored, then return to your work, while the stone remains hard.
de hernie carnouse	regarding fatty hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef; et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit .i. autre oef; et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit; et ceu n’avient se poc non.	Gelatinous mucus is nothing else but a gathering of moisture or white pus, which exists within the coat of the kidneys, that contains the egg; and it's called 'pus', and there isn't any proper time when it's properly in the membrane of the egg if one considers there to be another egg. And this is the skin under the kidney containing the white pus we've mentioned; and it doesn't have its own space no.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the creation of this gelatinous mucus comes from weakness that affects the kidneys, and spreads that substance.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors: ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	And it doesn't come at all from hitting the kidneys, and that moisture has many colors: or it becomes yellowish like jaundice, or without redness, or black, or aqueous white, and this happens more frequently.
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, .i. poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And these are the signs to recognize this assembly, for if it is or white and opaque as we have said, then the pus is present, .i.e. long like an egg figure, and does not open through the veins, because there is moisture everywhere inside.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if he has moisture in the proper tissue, then the pus is present with part of an egg, and based on this assumption it seems that there's another egg;
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien; donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	And if the moisture is between the skin of the veins and the white as said, you will feel it well; thus when you see the color of the moisture, try it on the entire square inside, from which the form was just described.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	Following this then, who comes after the introduction, judge by what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors; puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	And when we cure it with iron, the patient must be treated according to our ability and the strength of their body; then let them sit on their back, on something slightly elevated, and place wool beneath them;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des .ij. costelz dou keur des coions;	Then sit to the left side, and command the attendant to sit on the right, stretching their arm out along one of the two ribs towards the kidneys;
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	Then take the spatula and scrape the skin of the kidneys between them from head to tail until past the elbow, making a straight cut along the skin of the kidneys up to the white flesh, and gently burn it with your skill;
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a .i. large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	Then make a hole through the moist skin of one and a half inches wide and remove all the moisture. Then put your fingers in it, and position the wet cloth upstream from that point; but do not touch the hair rootlets, only the moist skin. Carefully scrape everything or piece by piece off his chest until you do so skillfully, otherwise the water will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les .ij. leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the egg jumps over your work, then reset it in its place as soon as you have completed the water treatment; then join together the two halves of the hair rootlets with stitches, and treat it just like any other wound until it heals completely.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	And if you find the egg corrupted by another disease, then it is necessary that you tie up the vessels that are suspended, in case there's bleeding; then operate on the groin until under the suspension point, and remove the egg, and treat it as we have said before.
Et se aigue est assemblee en .ij. parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont .ij. ramices; si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	And if the wound is made up of two joined parts, know that they are two branches; if you handle the other part in the same way as you did the first equally, then let the blood out and place wet wool in the wound smeared with rose oil.
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les .ij. coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and place another layer of wet wool in wine and oil, and apply it over the two wounds, then cover with folded cloths, and bind them on like this across the entire bandage.
Puis pren .ij. drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil; et li autre dui chief sus les .ij. angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	Then take two cloths, and fold them with rough wool according to this pattern, having them joined by stitching in the waist of breeches, and one of the shoulders lays on the foundation up to the back, and the other at the arm's part; and the other double head on the two angles, and have everything assembled in the loop of the garter.
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes .i. cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	And never is this treatment of cautery with the size of iron, and you should take one fine fire cautery, and peel the skin off the joints, and heat it up as we have said, so that the white fluid contained in the water is revealed;
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Take the cautery according to this shape, and pierce the white fluid at the joints, and burn it with this fine fire cautery:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout; et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef; et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve; et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	And cut the skin in all manners that you can, until you remove everything; and make sure the fire does not touch the egg; know that this work is more beneficial; and be careful of the bleeding from cuts, and know how to manage the opening of veins;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	And if no obstacle occurs to you, or discharge of pus or bleeding or any other issue, then treat according to what hinders you, as was said previously.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai,	And if the patients are afraid and do not wish to undergo this work because of its horror, then perform a puncture, as I have told you, and it is that when you are well assured by the meanings we have said that watery moisture lies there.
si fai seoir le malaide sus .i. siege leveit; puis perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors; et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	And make the patient sit on a raised seat; then pierce the abscess in the part under it at the entire pus-filled area, and make the puncture long across the core; and let the exit of the pus be wide enough so that all the liquid can come out.
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	And place cotton on the site, and secure it, and leave it so that any pus drains out, then treat until the wound heals completely;
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant; et eslarge .i. poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés .vj. mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	And if the white cloth does not allow water to escape from the mouth of the wound, then it is necessary for you to insert a feather or the tool used to treat the water of ydropiques, as described previously; and make the wound wider by about an inch. And know that the water returns and gathers after about seven months or eight, and when she has gathered like before, in this way her days will pass.
de l’aposteme des coions	regarding the abscess of the testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that in the section of this branch there are several ways to act, because I believe it's better to leave it alone;
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	And I will tell you about the operation and the appearance of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions; et c’est par mout de cas.	So, I will say that many abscesses come from horns or in animals; and this happens by chance.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	This is to know by excess of sharp acidity and fever which spreads in the animal's body or through impact.
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors; et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	And the color of the abscess is similar to that of the horn; and there is no pain found, it is an abscess filled with pus.
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	And by chance there may be one abscess filled with blood and pus, and of a reddish hue, and it does not come from the heart or inflame veins.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it comes from the heart, if you know by the location of the abscess heat, when you press it with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	And it is not right for you to touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois,	That which is made of swelling veins can be known by its position when touched with your fingers,
et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	And can do very well on this manner, and on other similar cases;
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	And you should make the cut of the cord, then place the egg on top, and press hard with white force at this spot, and release the suspension from all sides of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the egg is already stuck with these newly born ones, then you should remove the egg, and do it like this.
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	And if it's towards the white or in that which is inside the veins, then you should release all this tension, and do it round-like.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the beginning of life is behind or near the tail, it is necessary for you to grasp it completely and remove the egg, as we have said.

de l’aposteme des coions	regarding the abscesses of the kidneys

de la routure dou syfac	from the rupture of the uterus
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The events of this branch occur through the division that leads to uterine rupture, or an expansion on the abdomen in the area of the kidneys, because the intestines descend from that rupture towards one of the testicles;
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces .ij. manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	And this rupture is either due to uterine rupture or the expansion of it, and these two methods of animal causes occur: through beating, jumping, barking, lifting the lump with force, or by similar actions;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	And when it is due to uterine expansion, symptoms occur gradually and over a long time, not coming suddenly;
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	And it is that the pus is even up to around the front, because the syphilitic affects the intestine.

And the symptoms are when it's due to the division of the syphilitic disease, causing a sudden pain at the beginning, and there appears pus in various forms near the skin, because of the release from the intestine and the body's response to the syphilis further down.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And the glands often descend with the intestine, and are retained within, causing great pain to the patient, especially when they are pressed.

Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the way of operating is that you command the surgeon to guide or lead the knife deep into the wound where the organ resides, if it can fit inside;

et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	And ask about your hands if there is any part of the intestine wrapped or white, thick and hard, and if you find no such thing, hold it back at the stomach;
puis pren une aguille ou il ait .i. gros fil fait de .x. filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions; aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait .iiij. filz;	Then take a needle or it be one large thread made of ten threads, and hold it in the posterior part of the white, thick and hard area, which is after the skin of the anus; after cutting, then clip out the parts that appear from the threads, until there are four threads.
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de .ij. pars;	Then join them one above the other in a manner of a cross, and bind the white thick area, as we have said that it is around the skin of the anus, with a strong thread of two parts;
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de .ij. pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	Then wrap the ends of the threads around them and bind them firmly with two parts, so that none of the needles that are threading through cannot enter into them, preventing any abscess formation;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc .ij. dois de celui, et aprés ces .ij. liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	And place the bandage in a straight line according to the first long length of two fists from that point, and after these two bands allow for some space which is about at the center of your chest near the navel, the size of one fist;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte; puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	And after all else according to the roundness that the egg bears; then cut in the area near the skin of the belly, until the cord and the baby's head do not move, as we said earlier.
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	Then apply wet wool in oil, and place it on the wounds, and apply the bandage that we have described.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And once the white part of the belly mentioned has been incised, after the cut, by concern for bleeding, apply cautery.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui; et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	For this happens many times, and let the string hang until it breaks by itself; and if it does not fall in time, then raise it with hot water, and place upon it what we have said, until it breaks.
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	Then continue treating the wound with other remedies, until it heals completely.
de hernie carnouse	of fatty hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch I never see anyone who dares to perform the iron treatment.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the old ones said that it is done like a branch assembled together with a twist, in such manner that you tie the vessels after trimming them lightly over the spot.
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient; et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then cut me too, and treat the abscess of him who works, until the vessels bleed; and treat it in such a way as we have said, while he is still alive.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus; et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	Never come to rupture within the abdomen, as we said, and open their insides; and do not allow any of the intestines to escape in the process, and if they do escape a little, repair them immediately;
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	and still, if it stays too long at this point, suspect the wound or the abscess, especially when the intestines start to come out;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	This happens through the expansion of the sycophant which is at the angles, as we have said, for it has been expanded, then softened and swelled up his limbs and opened.
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit; et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	And the treatment is done with cautery, as we have mentioned before; and it is also cured in this way by iron:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de .iij. dois;	And if the patient lies on their back between your hands, then lift their shoulder from the swelling according to its size as large as two fists;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	Then remove the sycophant that is under the skin where it follows, then take its place and put it in the open area of the sycophant.
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les .ij. leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	And he presses at the bottom of the belly, then cuts the two that appear from the symphysis above the navel, and cuts each one separately.
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	Then extract the part of the ribs, and do not touch near the symphysis nor stretch the membrane to anything else, just as I have shown you in treating the removal of intestinal worms;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies. Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	Then treat it using wound healing methods. And when you clean the wounds, if you cleanse and treat the wound until it heals.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The umbilicus is constrained and does not show up in the incision, and the cauterization is practiced in this area, and closer to salvation.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	from the softening of the skin around the anus
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir; et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil; puis assemble les .ij. levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a .iij. costures ou .iiij. fermement; puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Many times the skin around the anus becomes soft in some people, due to the softening of the contents inside and it is something to be seen; when you want to treat it, one should let the patient lie on their back, then take off the softened skin from the natural skin. Then join the two flaps together at a suture point, and if necessary, sew the excess softened skin in three or four sutures, or firmly in two. Then cut between the seams, and treat the wound like any other, until it heals, and then remove stitches from the skin that has been treated.
dou chastrement	with chastity
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre; et n’est necessaires fuer que por .ij. manieres: dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure; et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes. Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc .ij. manieres: ou par atraction, ou par fendure.  En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant; puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.  Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a .i. cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez; et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz; et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure; puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Know that chastity is prohibited in our law, and because of this I would prefer not to speak about it in this book; and they are necessary only for two reasons: one being that the master needs to respond when someone asks him about it and how to treat it; and the other because we often need to apply chastity to some animals to help us, such as sheep and goats and cattle and others. Thus, then I say that chastity is done in two ways: either by attraction or by incision. When we do it through attraction, let the animal bathe in hot water until its anus softens and becomes wet; then take hold of it with your hand until it recovers and you no longer feel it. As for the tail whipping, you should mark the animal, press the anus skin with your left hand, then tie the scrotum, and treat each testicle separately when they have been well scraped; and leave no small hole or the subtle hole that is located in the veins; this method of chastity differs from the one done by attraction because there might be something left behind in the anus due to attraction which makes the animal lustful; then cure the wound until it heals.
des hermofrodites	Concerning hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc .ij. manieres as homes: l’une si est que entre les .ij. coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.  Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et .ij. coions.  Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies; en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	Hermaphrodites can be divided into two ways: one where between the two openings they are as in nature for a woman, having hair, and sometimes excreting urine. And another way is like in women, with something above the wrist resembling a penis and two openings. And in treating them you take all the joined parts, and treat them just like other wounds; in the second way, for men whose urine jumps through the skin of the openings, there's no treatment needed.
de la tentigene	Of the pustule
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir; et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure. Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement; et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee». Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	Tentigene is a joined spot on the natural body, such that it's too ugly to see; and some women have it as large as a hand, and this needs treatment. It is necessary that you color the excess of the tentigene with your thumb or underarms, and remove it gently; and don't clean it too much so that bleeding doesn't occur, then treat it again until it heals; and from another spot that arises at the mouth of saliva, and eat, and by chance burns, and resembles a cow according to its appearance, and for this they called it the old 'cow disease'. It is necessary that you remove it like we said about tentigene, and treat it until it's healed.
de erratique	Of the cautery by fire, command the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis; et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est; ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit; et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir; et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile. Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait. S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as .ij. leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi: met tes .ij. dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes; puis estent les .ij. leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens; puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder. Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte. Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope; et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef; puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder; et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec; puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.  Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez. Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	Erratic is when the nature of the woman isn't fully known, or if there's an excess or deficiency; it's natural by birth, or as accidents happen through illness that has come upon her; or due to bodily fluids being joined improperly, or owing to subtle or thick syphilis, and this occurs in front during marriage, on the ribs, underneath, wherever it may be; and one must understand its conception, childbirth, and sometimes floral reproduction; knowing this requires knowledge of the midwife. When the abnormalities are noticeable and apparent, they appear near your fingers or thigh area. If it's due to subtle syphilis, and it is close by the two lungs, then hurry, do like this: place your two index fingers together, and have the woman on her back, spread out her legs; then form the two lungs until the subtle syphilis is reduced, covering the abnormalities completely. Then take wool and fat in oil, put them over the area, and let the woman rest each day so that it doesn't bond. And if the syphilis is hard and thick, you must cover its appearance as if it were a leaf of rosemary. If the abnormalities are due to born flesh, then suspend her on her stomach and cover; use bandages with blood-stopping medicines such as arnica, dragon's blood, incense, all together in abundance with eggs; then make a plaster wide enough so that the wound can't bond; do this for an extended period, and cover it with a linen tent; then apply other treatments until healed. And when flesh is born during marriage if you need to cover according to this way, provided they aren't ingrown abscesses. For ingrown abscesses in the marriage area should not be touched by fire.
des emorroides	Of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul; et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation. Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer. Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer. Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses; puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide; et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai .i. emplaustre sus son dos. Et se il estainche, c’est boin. Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir; puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.  Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez; et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a .i. chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul; et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Wound openings are incisions in veins which occur without due caution and skill; when these wounds grow old they turn septic; we have mentioned in our division the signs, symptoms of this, and I will speak about those that heal through treatment. I state that septic wounds and the pus together, when they emerge from the mouth of the wound, do not show externally except for during treatment with iron. Wounds at the opening of the wound can be felt are those you can treat. Therefore, it is necessary to place the woman in a cool house, then make the pus ready on forceps and the root, then cover the area with medicine that restricts blood flow like cattail and dragon's blood and frankincense, among other things; then bind her feet for an hour, then place them in cold water; should there be bleeding from these, have her sit in a decoction of sumac bark, pomegranate peel, gall nuts and similar substances, then take wheat flour and mix it with honey and garlic, then make one plaster on her back. And if it stops bleeding, that is good. Should this not happen, should she develop abscesses on the back and nipples without cutting; then take wool, knead it into aloe juice or elderflower sap with old wine, and apply to her body.
des apostemes de la marris	The abscesses of the womb
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division. Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe; et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.  Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie; et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus .i. siege, et ait .ij. petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe; et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien; puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme; et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide; et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve; et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument. Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	Many ways of abscess come in the womb, such as gangrene, puerperal abscesses, herpes, indolent ulcers, fistulas, hemorrhoids and other abscesses I mentioned in our previous discussion. Therefore, it is necessary that I discuss here about the vaginal abscess which occurs in the womb, distinguishing it from those abscesses which harden and persist for a long time; if you see signs of illness in iron operations, observe whether the abscess is hot at the beginning of its appearance, and filled with fever and heat, and whether it turns red when you can see it. So do not rush to pierce it right away, but wait until the pain subsides completely; then have her lie on one side with two small stools under her hips so she is inclined, and support her back and legs together at the sides of her leg; let her knees be spread apart, place her arms under her knees, and bind them well with a bandage; then help the pus spill to the right side of her body, and apply the tool used for opening her womb from which the form comes; it is necessary that when you see this tool applied, make sure it enters about an inch into the womb so that what goes inside does not go too far beyond its place and does not hurt the patient; if the instrument is large, it should be covered with a bandage to prevent it from causing discomfort to the patient; it must hold the nozzle of the instrument above her and cut the instrument. And when the abscess opens up and you can handle it gently by hand, you must cover it with ointment until it dries out; then apply moistened wadding in oil rose or oil green; put the dressing at the bottom of the wound up to the edge of the womb, and place more clean, moistened wool under the womb on her back. de l’enfantement	Of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar: adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir; adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui; et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost; car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification; et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment. Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises; si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	The first task for the midwife is to recognize the form of natural childbirth, and the signs indicate when you see the woman's belly enlarge, and desire to smell her: then the child begins to exert force to come out; thus you know that this birth takes place according to its natural form, and occurs from its head, and the second part with it; and when you notice these signs, gently pressing on their abdomen is necessary so that the child comes out soon; for when it descends through its head, the second part accompanies it, and is born free of its excesses by good cleaning; any other birth does not come naturally. For it appears sometimes from its feet, and emerges through force of the body or limbs, or hands, or from her abdomen, or stomach, and is turned by chance around its neck, and by other bad forms; herein it is necessary for the midwife to be wise and subtle in these matters, and beware of error and deception, and I will show you all the forms on how they should be assisted.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent; et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	When the child comes through its head by natural birthway, and the woman is in severe labor, and her strength is weak, she should be seated on a stool or held by women; then let her rise from this position where fenugreek was cooked, and then have the midwife place between her fingers the small spoon as shown below:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers; et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament; puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre: si istra maintenant l’enfes.Et se les .ij. mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc; et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus .i. siege, et li lieve les piés en haut; puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement; et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	And cut the second part, and remove until all the moisture that is within disappears; and pull out the belly of the woman as far as the child descends, and if it doesn't descend, it is necessary to give a woman a catheterization with fenugreek seed oil. Then make her drink and sniff consilium, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour: and let the child now come out. And if those two hands force their way out, you should gently pull them in one by one; and if they cannot enter, put the woman on a bench, and lift her feet upwards; then remove the bench from the ground, and cut under the woman so she does not leak during birth. And if the hands cannot enter and the child has died, cut the hands with the knife that was prepared beforehand, extract the child, and pull them out evenly.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piez	from the delivery of the child on her feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child comes down onto her feet, it's best to lift her up.
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then turn it slowly, little by little,
puis preigne .i. des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then place one of the ends and gently extend it little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	Can he jump up to his thighs, if commanded, and make him inhale cautiously with the command;
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	if he can jump, may God will it.

Car adonques ist il legierement.	Because then make it slightly easier.

de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	from the position of the child on his knees

de l’enfant mort	of the dead child

et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	And this is the form of the hair:

Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman who had borne one child that died, then she gave birth to another from that same womb, and this other also died.

dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring the shoulder back to its place

Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument with which one fumes a woman during retention of flowers and afterbirth is thus:

et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	Let there be fumigation above the coals, and let the treatment continue until it is exhausted, then start another one.
de percier lou fondement	To puncture the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Newborns are born who do not have immediate perception, instead they perceive through a subtle sense.

And if you doubt that it won't reoccur, put or insert a piece of poplar wood, and leave it in the person's mouth for days, and remove it when the child begins to walk around indoors.
