de la fistule dou fondement	from the fistula from its base
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	Fistulas that come from beneath the foundation are congealed and grow larger; those that come from above the foundation or in the space of two parts,
si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe,	If there is one fistula or multiple; and when that congealed mass is old, it works and absorbs moisture, yielding white or fine pus,
et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And there are no times these Persian fistulas; and they're known by the fact that there's either discharge or windiness when the patient discharges, and perhaps in jumping from one place to another.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And there are fistulas that penetrate up to the bladder, and up to half of the penis; they reach up to the joint of the knee, and up to the root of the testicles.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one can recognize a Persian fistula at its base, but not necessarily Persian.
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	And you should touch the end of your index finger or base, and insert a slender needle or spider's leg or iron into the fistula when there is no twist.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it is twisted, you should hold up a thread of fine wax or one horsehair until you feel the thread or hair at your hand;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	And if you don't feel it, and there is no full evacuation of pus, wind, or air, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	Know that it does not harm; if you hasten to heal.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula is close enough to the bladder or where urine leads, if it jumps with urine and cannot be sealed by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it penetrates up to the knee joint, then there is a vein going up to that point;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is no winding or the cause of pain is within, then it remains inside and cannot be treated with medicine or ointment.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And for these Persian fistulas there is no remedy but labor, and vain effort of those who interfere with them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit,	And in those that are not Persian nor ancient, there is hope for healing through iron, as I have found out.
et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	And when the patient lies on their back in your hands; and raise their legs up to their hips, and have their hips tilted towards their stomach.
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then insert an arachnid tentacle, or if there's curvature, a diving bell until you know where the tentacle comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice,	If they feel the pain deep inside, it is necessary for you to push your index finger there,
se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	Then you will sense that the tool has pierced it; and know where its entry or the artery or the vein lies beneath your finger, so you'll understand whether it's in an artery or a vein.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If there is no disturbance, one cannot examine it.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	Yet still, with a little effort, one can often examine some things, but this happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	And when we assist, if we warm the delicate cautery according to the width of the fistula, as was explained before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and pour heat it entirely in the fistula until it emerges from the foundation; and do this twice or three times, until you know that these heated parts are burnt, which resemble a bird's feather;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then treat the moistened wicks with grease, until this heated part comes out, then apply ointment to bind and fuse it.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If it is done like that, it is fine. Otherwise, it cannot be treated in any other way;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	And if it is attempted to be inserted within, and does not penetrate until the base which is the foundation, and between your thumb and the tent there is a thick covering of flesh or of fat, and you can see the fistula in the one who has created this covering deep inside.
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	if the operation is done at the beginning of the fistula, stops firmly before the tent, and then uses the cautery afterwards, until it reaches the tip of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	and removes the tent, and it will fall out; then remove those fat lumps that seem like a bird's feather, and do not leave any remnants.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the wound does not heal, cut between you and the organ, then apply fire or an ointment to treat it.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	For fire cautery combines two substances: this is to say, the burn of these iron rods arranged together, and the extinguishing of blood and the drying of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then the treatment of wet tents involves rubbing or grinding them in butter or on objects until the wax flows out, and it releases the burned parts within the wax;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then treat the wound with black soldering operations that harden over time, and use dried medicines as remedies.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	And when it has been restored, if it is healed and does not recur.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes just short of the full bottom, and is removed from the body, you should tap on its base or bottom, and inquire about it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	And if you feel the tentacle, and there are two of it or something soft like a string or cord, or it's about to pierce, but there is only a path of entry and hope, by applying one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you apply cautery as we have said, or you cut it up to the bottom, or if you can feel and remove it like the first one does.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and don't cut too close to the bottom, that you might remove what holds the base, and allow it to be expelled naturally by the body.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then the treatment, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	by chance if it is healed, or you remove that covering and clean it since it has been cut from under the root, either by mistake or with another instrument pointed.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then cleanse that wound flesh which is in the injury as much as you can.
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	then strive to heal the wound, and keep the hole open in the lower part of the root: if it is easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And no way are fistulas according to this manner: and when you pinch the tent in the fistula, and it's where the base touches the skin above,
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	if you take a tent pierced at the head following this form:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And tie one twisted thread in a knot, and pinch the tent throughout the whole length of the thread in the fistula until it reaches the head.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If she is passing through the base in the margin inside, then pull out that thread from the twisted one as you pinch your thumb or base.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	And guide the head with thread, and join the two heads together, and hold one against the other, and let it rest for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	And hold them tight every time until the threads reach these parts that are between the two heads, and keep joining them together.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	Then treat the wound until it is healed and clean.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not burst, make an incision in all ways that you can, as long as it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not fitting to do so by laying the patient flat immediately, and then treating them, as we have said, until they are stabilized.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the sharp-pointed needle used for making a puncture is much like this, and it involves cutting;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	And on another side, no, because you should not touch what you should not touch, as you see here:
des emorroydes	of lacerations
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Fatigue occurs in two ways: when they are within the foundation, like a piece of tar, and if there are small and large ones, and blood collects at that spot.
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	and one or more of them are outside the foundation and under the root; but those that are out have little moisture.
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	and also at that spot a little yellow water or a little blood, and they have the color of the flesh;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and for those who have them within the foundation, you instruct the patient to move around in chambers so that the foundations come out and the threads are visible.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you're quick, pinch it with your tweezers, or hold it by your nail, then pull at its roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	And if the ring can't hold onto them due to their moisture, take them at two inches apart, or with cotton, or from a piece of metal;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	And pull them off with your fingers, then apply it, and dust it with some hot powders that would be used for a cauterizer;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	Or you can cauterize them as it is said or as the chapter on cauterization instructs, then treat with other remedies until they are healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	And if the foundations cannot come out, then direct the patient to perform lithotomy using a sharp and abrasive tool to wash away whatever is on the foundation, so that it can come out smoothly;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	And if the patient's efforts are not effective in the opening and if the threads are strong at the foundation, then the treatment should be light;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And when you grasp them with your finger or tweezers, remove them, then treat in the manner we have described, until it is clean and it dreads iron incision.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	It is necessary for you to suture in this manner: take a twist of thread and put it into a needle, then pull the thread over and make a hole in the needle from another side, and turn the two ends of the thread under the needle.
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	And if it is broad; and hold the thread in place, then tie the thread, sew with the needle, remove the needle, do this for all others, and leave one out to manage excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place on the base one part of moist lint in olive oil or on a wadding, and place on the base, then instruct the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And leave it until they heal completely, and when they are settled, perform treatment with ointment and other remedies, as long as they are healing.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	By drying heat or the base.
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times, there is dryness of bile in the intestines, and due to nature's constraint, and when the illness is old and medicine no longer helps.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It is necessary that you reset at the tip of a spur or on your nail, leaving no moisture;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then apply the heat until it becomes soft as required;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	And if it doesn't become soft, repeat the operation with more force than before, until some healing occurs and it is scorched;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat him as long as he remains healthy.
dou fremit	with tremor
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Ants is a small false appearance on the body, and they move everywhere.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And it never lets you feel the vein when pressed, and one also feels its death like a tremor, spreading throughout the body, especially more in the hands than other parts.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a twig from an goose feather or a strong vulture feather and place this stick over the trembling (area), until the reddish circles cover the whole trembling region.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand until you grasp the entire stick as long as you cover all of the trembling (area), and place it forward, and root out the trembling from its source.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see fit, do this with a twig of an araign or iron according to this shape, and make it subtle underneath and taut above:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	Do not pierce it, for you must hold onto the two ends and apply pressure. And if you see fit, cauterize the trembling (area), as is shown or described in the chapter about cauterization.
de la forme dou clistere	of the bladder's structure
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	Never use an argentin or archaut bladder, or one made of melted silver or lead; and never use small or large utensils depending on who they are for.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore, those utensils should be used in the treatment of children and those who are weak and painful, as they are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The shape of the bladder is either small or large, just like this:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	And there is a protrusion where the belly button is sewn closed, as you can see, and feces are inside piercing it; and on one side of the abdomen there are two depressions, and on the other one.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	And let it be that the belly is where I place medications from a beast bladder or parchment, and it should have tiny depressions pierced through it all around.
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	And place exactly one inch between each depression, then insert two strands of strong, twisted thread into these depressions for ten or twelve times around, and bind the belly as tightly as a goat would.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	And when the medication is inside, tie it with a strong thread in front of the tool, then stitch it; and this forms a circle.
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine neither be too hot nor too cold, and smear the head with oil or yolk of egg ointment, or something similar, then gently rub it in.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	Then, with the surgeons at his two hands together, until he sees clearly, then remove the lump, and lift the patient's legs onto the table.
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	And if the medicine is to come out, let it escape as much as possible; and if he sleeps through a night, that will be more help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you administer it during a colicky disease of the stomach, and the medicine rushes to escape, then repeat it as long as he is well.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if bleeding occurs from its root or its source, or from an abscess, even a cyst as small as one child;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the shape of the thin cyst on which the skin is constrained:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have spoken about the treatment of wounds in our division; now we will speak about treatments for hands and medicine, according to completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are various depending on how they are made, and where the wounds are made, and why they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The reasons wounds are made include impact from a stone, the size of a sword and a knife, or by a spear or a staff or a mace, or by similar things.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or depending on the location of the body, such as a wound inflicted upon the neck, or the head, or the stomach, or the abdomen, or the liver, and similar parts.
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and start with wounds of the head that are simple, because the memory refers to its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	I say that when a single wound occurs or when bone fractures, and the bone is not broken, be cautious if it's due to stone or similar conditions, and the skin has been completely torn and the wound is large,
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	and you doubt slightly about abscesses: if the surgeon immediately cleans the head wound even if there is a little blood from the wound, and the treatment goes against the part that was removed;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	and encourage the patient to drink plenty of wine and eat rich meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he doesn't want to undergo surgery, then reduce his food intake, and do not drink wine or eat meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	And if there's pus coming out of the wound, when you find an abscess, place a wet cotton ball in oil rose water or just oil; or in vinegar that stops bleeding.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	And if there's no pus coming out of the wound, when you place it on the wound, if it contains fresh blood throughout and isn't disturbed by air, a powder that I will mention shortly;
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound has been disturbed, apply some ointments until it heals.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large like a cut from a sword and similar injuries, and the edges cannot be brought together by sutures, then join them with stitches, as I will say for abdominal wounds, regarding suture.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound exposes the bone, and there's tenderness, yet it only lasts for a short time when touched, then one must treat; then heal the wound with medicine, and restore hard flesh instead of skin.
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	And instruct the patient to eat large meats, such as kidneys and cooked wheat, like chickens, and similar items.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find that the skin is rotting, and it doesn't reach to the bone, then cut out the whole rot, and remove the pus, then treat;
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is an artery in the wound or vein, which cannot be stopped with medicine, then cut off the artery, and if you find it dislocated, tie it with a thread;
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if this does not benefit you, then apply cautery to it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if the wounds are small and simple, then the treatment is light: and you should put this powder which joins together like that when the heat of the fire has moved it.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And here is the way to prepare the powder: take a part of frankincense; dragon's blood two parts; powdered galium three parts, and finely ground it.
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	Apply the wound, pressing it firmly until it is well aired and joins with all its blood;
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	And then it must be properly aligned, and left untouched until it heals, if it doesn't swell; for the medicine is not removed as long as it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And one should only perform this bloodletting procedure once, not just because of the need for charcoal or dragon's blood, but when the surgeon has cleaned the wound.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the surgeon has treated the wound, in that state, one should not apply this powder at all;
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	Instead, apply some digested ointments, or oat flour mixed with water and honey, until the wound starts to heal;
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then continue with other treatments as long as they are healthy.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if bone breaking comes with the wound, and it is small, treat it with fine tweezers;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	And I will tell you later about the fractures of the head.
de la plaie dou col	of the wound in the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	This injury comes from the neck, it is simple if there's no distinction between the neck and the head itself, but if the nerves in the neck or an artery has been severed.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it's the nerves, then leave the treatment alone and don't put anything that restricts, for it harms the nerves and makes them recede;
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	And don't place anything cold on the wound, for the substance of nerves is cold and they continue with the head which is among the highest parts.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	but use warm medicine instead, such as rose water rinsed with gentle water, and rinse the cabbage leaves also in gentle water,
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	And other stones within according to this manner, and moist applications.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, one should bend the edges and let it heal until it is clean.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and filled with pus, one should pierce them or lower further.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	And if the artery is cut and bleeding ensues, one should open it, bandage it, and then cauterize where necessary;
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	And if the throat's flesh is cut, or the kidneys, and the passage is kept maintained, through which the meat goes,
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	if you make a cut in the kidney over the reed of the throat, and not touch the throat but set it according to its natural form;
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then allow for healing, and leave it for some days, then treat with dried ointments until it heals properly;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if the wound has affected the bone, treat that as well;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	And if there are bone fragments, remove them all thoroughly if you can, and those that you cannot obtain, allow the wound to heal until it is clean.
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	and make sure the dislocation is corrected and stable.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	And if the wound is fresh, apply the powder I mentioned.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there are bones in the wound and it has a sinus, treat it as described in my chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	From the wound caused by a spear or knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it's from a spear or knife, and the wound goes deep, if you observe that the air escapes through the wound without any resistance from the body: then you know that the wound is mortal;
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	And if it's not deep and all its blood is fresh escaping freely, then don't delay to put the powder at first hour or don't bind it for fear that the blood might stop flowing completely.
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	And tend to his heart, and rest the patient;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but apply an attractive ointment, and bind it twice daily;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you don't have an ointment, place old cotton in the wound to absorb the moisture,
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	let the patient rest on the wound for three days, or four, or more if necessary;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	if no convulsions, bad heart tremors, or alone jumps occur;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	And when you see the good conditions, if you know that the wound is saved.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then cure it with various remedies and other treatments, as long as it remains healthy;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	And if it cannot heal properly and heals unevenly, then you will realize that there is an ulcer; treat it accordingly.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or knife cut and it's straightforward or worse, or on the back, treat it in accordance with that which comes before.
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	If it's large, stitch it; and if it's small, use powder, and if it's compressed in the bone, and has fractured pieces, clean the wound, and remove the debris if they are exposed.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	And if they aren't exposed, leave the wound to heal open, letting ease the extractions;
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	and for other wounds on other limbs, make judgments as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	about the rupture of the abdomen
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The belly depressions are large and medium-sized and small;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	From a large wound, once the intestines or the ends of the intestines, through which the invasion occurs;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	And the suture is more difficult, and no time matches worse than a small wound compared to a large one,
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	Because in this way, we can't place the intestines properly inside, unless we put them back little by little.
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	Because when their intestines swell up as soon as they feel the cold, they go back inside more points,
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	And because of this the patient sweats from the wound, for this is when we move their intestines back to where they belong, like in the case of others two.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	Know that there are four ways a stomach rupture occurs:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	the two common stitches occur in the abdominal area,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	And the stitching of other wounds on the body, and two other types of stitches for their own purposes, are common to other wounds;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	And yet, they are more proper with the stitch on the belly, and I will mention each one and explain them.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small, and nothing of the intestine sticks out,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	and when there is something to remove, this can be done in either of two ways:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	because of the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or because the intestines are swollen due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, warm him up in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	moisten a sponge or make one part of a cloth wet only in water,
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	when you cook with boiling water mixed with soap and thyme,
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and let the intestine swell as long as it is perforated;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	and after doing this with straining wine, and when it has been cooked, allow it to cool so that the swelling may subside.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see the swelling disappear, moisten the intestine with water or broth that has been cooked and flavored.
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	Because with this there is difficulty at the beginning of things;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	and if it cannot enter, they make a small incision with the tool that removes the moirants;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	And the first treatment is to have it bruised by the cut,
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	And we should not cut it without great necessity, nor if there's no alternative;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	And these are the tools to split them:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if you cut inside the bend and not outside, and see this shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound is enlarged, and the intestines jump out,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	if you reset it according to its natural form in its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	if you can do so, for this requires movement.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is wide, and it's in the abdominal area,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	if necessary, heal the patient on their back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	And place his legs higher than his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	and if it is in the abdominal region,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	then position the head and the buttocks higher than the abdominal area.
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and also if there is a rupture in the abdomen at one of these two parts.
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	if you understand this, let the part that has been removed be higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	and thus should practice what I say in large and medium-sized wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	For small wounds, use what you are equipped for,
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	Then have in your hands a minister of pity who heals the entire wound with its hand,
et assemble les levres;	And gather the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	and this is the common method of stitches,
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	and you take one or more needles, according to the size of the wound's width,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	then leave at the start of the wound an inch in space, and I insert a needle or it has one good thick thread;
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	and pierces the two skin heads with the two bone heads,
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	who are underneath the skin inside, until you pierce that part of it.
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and connect the two bone heads with the four assembly;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then tighten a double thread around the needle of those two parts,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	then gather together both of the ends of the wound extension,
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	and then leave an inch of space, and insert another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then tie the thread in the same way you did with the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and keep doing this according to your skill with the needles,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until all the wound remains restrained;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	and have equal needles, both fine and thick,
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	because the fine needles cut all the flesh, and the too thick ones cannot enter well:
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	thus they should be of medium thickness;
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	And it is not right to pull out the needles too far from the flesh and skin.
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	And they do not rupture or open the wound before the seam;
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	Then remove the heads of the needles, so that they do not irritate the patient at night;
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	And place tents or cloths over the joints of the needles to keep them in place;
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	And let them grow until the wound has healed;
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	And this kind of stitch using needles is more suitable for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	because it involves threading a needle or two.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second type of stitch is common,
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	And it is that you assemble the two sides of skin and the two sides of bone together on one needle where there is a strong thread in the middle;
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	and when you have pierced these four pieces together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	then remove the needle from where you began, in the way one sews linens;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and leave a distance between each stitch equivalent to the size of a small thumb.
ceste costure sevent li home,	This stitch sews up the wound,
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	and I sew a wound where someone had an injury or stomach issue,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	which was caused by a knife cut,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and the wound was larger than a palm in size,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	And if they are of intestines well two palms of great size,
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	And it was a wound in the middle of the belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I returned the intestine to him after it had been out for twenty-four hours.
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	And the wound was healed until fifteen days, and I treated it, and he was healthy.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And when they had judged that he was dying, and this was a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and did not cure him with ointment, for I was in one place where none could be found, nor any medicine;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	and changed the gauze on the wound four times a day, and washed it with honey water until it healed.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	And I will tell you the two proper ways of suturing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle, and the bottle from the outer part up until it reaches inside.
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	When she has pierced straight to the heart in the right place, if it hits the head of the syphilitic sore or causes pain or where you have stuck the needle,
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	and make her pierce from the inner part outwards until she reaches the outer side;
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	and if you hear that stitch, do it in such a way as the leatherworker sews the skin,
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	And you allow once the stitch on one side, and take it again from another, until the suture is fully completed.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second method of stitching, as Galen truly described,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	If it is like what everyone does, joining the two parts naturally together,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	And they press one end of the stitch to the other, in this manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	Prick a needle or take some medicine near the head of the dog, and pierce that spot alone.
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	and let both shoulders move smoothly.
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	then twist the needle, and pierce it from below up to that inner part,
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	similarly with both shoulders being in place;
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	Then pierce both from the lower part up to that within, in two other dislocated shoulders that are on the other side;
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	And this is the way of sewing that is moved and the more common one.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	The doctors say this word and none testify to it,
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	One should stitch the abdomen with two needles, or where there is thread in each;
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	And one must push a needle from one side, and the other from the other, in the manner of those who sew buttons;
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	Know that when the rupture is within the belly,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	The stitching there is more dangerous than for any other part of their belly.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgments about the wound are such as for the judgments of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	And it is that when you find the wound fresh with all its blood, as soon as the art has mixed it,
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	if it comes back into the intestine, and on the skin; then place the powder stimulating flesh,
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	and if the art has mixed it, apply any available unguent until the wound heals;
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	and clean the thread, and stitch up the cut, and bind it with a cloth.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat the wound as usual, until it stops bleeding;
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	and if you don't have medicine, place some, as soon as it starts to ooze pus, old cotton,
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	and move him twice a day until it stops bleeding.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you need no other medicines in various preparations for simple wounds;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	And if you doubt whether the wound will spread to the main parts of the body,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	Then it is necessary for you to moisten fine wool in oil that has been heated to a moderate temperature, or in scented oil,
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and place it inside the joints, and over the elbows;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	and if you feel pain or gangrene in your limbs, and such symptoms occur repeatedly,
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	If you use black wine enemas, and particularly if there is already gangrene reaching to the intestine;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	And pierce deeply inside, and know that when it comes to the large intestines, it is easier to heal than the smaller ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestine called 'juvenile' cannot be healed if it is injured,
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	And this is due to the location of the veins and because of the subtlety of the entire body, and its proximity to its nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the pus jumps out of the wound, then replace it immediately as with an intestine, while it is still fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	and if it is old and turned red or black, then you should bind the part that has become black so that no blood flows there,
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	because there are veins and arteries involved;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	then remove the one between the bandage,
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	And have both of those shoulders hanging down from the upper part over the wound up to beyond it for easing the extraction when the thorns pierce through, and the wound heals.
de la routure dou boueil	Of the rupture of the bladder
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are involved, and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	If it can be restored in any way,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	For I saw that someone was pierced or stabbed in the belly with a spear;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	and the wound was on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and it became inflamed and turned into a fistula, causing both loss of appetite and nausea;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I treated him according to what I knew, and didn't stop refining the treatment until he recovered, and bound his wounds.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw it fastened [securely], I doubted whether the patient might have pain in their belly;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	and there was no harm, but remained in better conditions, eating and drinking;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	and some experimenters say that when there is a small injury in the intestine, it should be bound in this manner:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	take large thorns, then gather the edges of the wound,
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	And when the bird has opened its mouth, you place it on the two lips,
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	if it stretches its mouth out;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	and then grasp its head, and this is held so that it cannot escape.
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	then place another bird in the same manner as before, until the wound has been completely covered.
et cout la plaie.	And at the wound site.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	If it burns strongly in the intestine, and causes no harm to the patient,
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	And one can tie the intestine with a thin thread cut from an animal's intestine,
en teil maniere:	in this manner:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	Take the head of this thread-like intestine until you reach the part that is lean,
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	and then tie to the head of this thread-like strand, one inch of fine linen string,
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	then thread the string through a needle and sew the intestine, then reset it in the opening;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	and this method of sewing like stitches is solely according to the way of joining and expecting;
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	And if the wound is big and wide, especially when it's in one of the bowels, if there's no fetus or health issue, because of subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	of a fistula, or where it might be.
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	Know that any wound or abscess, as it matures, is universally called "fistula".
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	And similarly when it is filled with hair and grows inside.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	And fistula is according to the white hard bulge of the improperly removed node, or where no pain can be felt,
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	and also has hair like the feathers of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	nor does it ever have clear vision, and at other times thickened vision.
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	neither is it ever too little, nor is there enough at other times;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	And I have spoken about it in the section on wounds, that any wound that is not healed, and there's no flesh,
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	This is only due to one of the eight causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	This means, it's because of the weakness or obstruction of blood or pus;
ou por sa malice;	or due to its maleficence;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	Because there is hard flesh within, and on the lips, which does not allow for hair to grow;
ou il i a trop de bowe;	because there is too much moisture;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	or the joints are swollen, and the substance is of poor quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	or the medicine is not good in the treatment;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	because corruption is a manner of pestilence;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	or because the property in the region is late for digestion, and its restoration is slow, and it escapes by nature;
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	or there are veins or bones:
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	and I have shown all these causes, and the signs, and the treatments with medicine in this section.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	It is necessary for me to inform you about the treatment of fistula, which is performed by manual work.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that a fistula can occur in all limbs and trunk;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	because there are fistulas that come from large veins, and arteries, and nerves,
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	or in the stomach, or in the intestines, or in the bladder, or in any of the ribs,
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	In the spinal column of the back, or at any joint of the hands or feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	And if it concerns the property of the main limb, and to its various functions.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all the fistulas in this manner are difficult to heal, and there is nothing else but hard work, and lack of knowledge;
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure,	and if there is no fistula that does not stop at the point I have said, and you are to complete the treatment,
et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	And you will know it, if you take a spider's tent or iron, if the fistula is straight, then touch it;
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc,	and if the fistula is curved, look for a subtle snail shell to probe it.
car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	for snails bend and move along the curvature;
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes,	and if the fistula has no means of hands and you cannot properly search for it with spider tents,
si la clisterize par l’un des pertus,	if you cleanse using one of the small tubes,
car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	for moisture is limited between one tube and another, and it cleanses;
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont,	then carefully probe with your strength, knowing if there is bone or nerve, and feel it all around,
et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	and ask the patient to describe where they feel pain when you press their hand, and determine the exact location.
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine,	And when you truly know its location, and if it is far from a joint, or a nerve, or an artery or vein,
ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit,	or in any of the joints that I have told you about, if there is pressure according to what I have told you,
et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	and when bone has been excavated and the putrefied flesh that is inside;
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee,	and then continue the treatment until it is healed.
et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues,	And if the fistula is well deeply opened straight ahead, it must be closed completely from top to bottom as much as you can,
puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule,	Then I apply moistened wicks to the ague medicine, and dab until reaching the tip of the fistula,
tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	Until the medicine dissolves what has remained at the bottom;
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then I cover it with clean bandages until it heals;
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit,	And if one cannot heal him with this, then apply the cautery as we have said.
et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	And if the bone is corrupted by the fistula, then treat it.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	If a vein or nerves are being harmed or affecting principal members, as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee,	And if the bone is exposed, and there's corruption and darkness, then treat it until all the corruption has been removed, as we have said;
puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then the surgeon cuts away the flesh as long as there is sound tissue;
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant,	and if it is not sound, cut around it in the same way as before,
saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	know that you should stop just at this point:
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons,	if it continues and grows to the bottom, continue cutting until you reach the bottom.
et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	And remove all the corruption, then reset it;
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	And if it is like this healthy, that's well.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	But if not, know that the corruption has gone too far within, and you cannot bring it back;
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	yet there is no other way than to leave it to nature;
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles,	And if there is a tiny bone corrupted, you may pull it out with tongs.
si l’estrai a .i. estrument covenauble a ceu,	if you find an instrument suitable for this task, extract it.
et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	and if there are many bones, remove them all, do not leave any behind;
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour,	and if moisture opposes this, and there is no fear or danger,
si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	If there is heat and moisture and flesh, and frees the bones.
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture,	And if you cannot remove them within an hour, then place something that resists putrefaction over the wound,
et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os,	and leave it until the flesh is completely putrid inside the bones,
et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	and then the bones will come out more easily;
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse,	And if it's a large bone, like from the leg or thigh,

puis restoure la plaie;	then heal the wound;
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	and if there is a large part of corruption and it extends up to the bone's surface;
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	If necessary, you should shave and cover it all until decay occurs, and then treat it as long as it is healing;
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint .i. home en sa jambe,	and I will tell you about a fistula that occurred in one's leg.

Il fut .i. jovencelz entor .xxx. ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors,	There was once a young person around thirty years old, who experienced pain in their leg due to an issue originating within the body,
tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	Until the substances reached the leg, and was drained of a large abscess, and there was no reason to open further;
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri,	but the doctor due to his zeal opened as much as the abscess allowed,
et en corroient mout de matieres, et devint fistule, et i vint mout de pertus que tuit gitoient bowe et moistor dou cors;	and did not remove much material, and became a fistula, and a great deal of pus was released that all flowed with the body's moisture;
et maint mire i mirent cure entor .ij. ans, et n’i ot nul saige en l’art de mains,	and many doctors spent two years treating him, and there was no wise one in the art of hands,

et devenoit rouges li cors dou jouvenceil, et avoit color citrine.	and his face turned red like a child's cheek, and it had a yellowish color.
Je boutai une tente en l’un de ces pertus, et puis cerchai toz les pertus,	I set up my tent in one of these veins, and then searched all the veins,
et trovai que li uns venoit encontre l’autre de toutes les parties de la jambe.	And I found that one was coming against the other from all parts of the leg.
Je me hastai donques, et copai en l’un des pertus tant que je descovri une partie de l’os,	So I hurriedly acted, and made a cut on one of the protrusions until I uncovered part of the bone,
et le trovai corrumput et perciet, et venoit li corruption jusc’a l’os dedens;	and I found it corrupted and perforated; and the corruption was reaching into the bone;
je soiai ceu qui m’aparissoit de l’os corrumput, et cuidai qu’il n’i eust autre corruption, fuer que celi que je ostai;	I saw what appeared from the corrupted bone, and I thought that there was no other corruption, only this one that I had taken;
et comensai a restourer la plaie de medicines sodans par lonc tens, et ne pot souder;	And began to restore the wound using long-term medicine treatments, and was unable to heal;
et puis rencomensai, et descovri l’os si com devant,	and then restarted, discovering the bone just as before,
et trovai la corruption continuee en l’os, et la soiai, et puis l’ostai, et me penai de souder le leu;	I found that the decay had continued in the bone, and I saw it, and then I took out the bone, and I tried to heal the wound;
mais je ne pou tant que je copai entor une palme de l’os, et le traï fuer a tout son mole,	but I was unable to do so as long as I copied just one palm of the bone, and I made it go to all its extent,
puis le restourai de medicines; et il fut sanez et soudez hastanment,	Then he will recover with medicine; and it healed quickly.
et ne covint plus rencomencier l’ovraige fors por la foibleté dou malaide, qui ne pooit soffrir,	and there was no need to start the operation again except for the weakness due to the patient's illness, who could not endure it.

Car por l’evacuation sanglotoit sovent, mais il fut sanez entierement,	But because of the blood evacuation was frequent, yet he healed completely,
et nasquit en leu de l’os une char dure, et fut de bone disposition et n’ot point de nuisement ne de contraire dou tout en tout, ne a l’aleir ne a venir.	And from within the body of the bone comes forth a tough flesh, and it is well arranged and has no harm or opposite effect at all in any part, neither near nor distant.
Et se li os est brisiez en aucun leu dou cors, si le covient soier en ceste maniere:	And if the bone breaks anywhere in the body, it should be treated in this manner:
pren .i. liien, et l’estrain au chief de l’os qui apert,	Take one ligament and stretch it to the tip of the broken bone,
et comande aucun k’il l’estende en haut;	and command him not to stretch it upwards;
et met .i. autre lien de lainne plus gros dou premier liien, et le lie sus la char qui est desor l’os,	And put another piece of wool cord larger than the first one, and tie it above the flesh that is around the bone,
et estent le chief, si que tu traies la char corrumpue au desoz,	And extend the head, so that you can pull out the decayed flesh from below.
et descuevre la char sus le leu ou tu vues soier, que li soie ne blece la char;	And uncover the tissue at its place where you see silk, making sure the silk does not hurt the tissue;
et met .i. tison ou une tauble desoz l’os por mues coper la char corrumpue;	And put a piece of charcoal or a board under the bone to warm up and cover the decayed flesh;
et covient tant soier com on puet veoir et sentir la corruption, et soier ancor autre fois.	And it is necessary to know as much as one can see and feel the decay, and know again otherwise.

et puis soie des l’une partie a l’autre la corruption, et soit li soieure dou lonc de la corruption .i. poc, si com nos avons dit;	and then apply the healing to each part of the corruption, and make sure the hot iron is long enough to cover the length of the corruption, as we have said;
et se li corruptions est en la jointure, si cope la jointure corrumpue, et soie l’os ou elle contient de l’autre part;	And if corruption is at the joint, then fix the corrupted joint, and let bone on the other side contain it;
et se li corruptions est en la continuation des .ij. jointes, si n’i a autre angien que dou coper;	And if corruption is along the continuity of the two joints, then cope it if there's no other way to do so;
et se li corruptions est ou poignil de la main, ou ou poignil dou piet, si est mout fort celle chose,	And if corruption is at the base of the hand or foot, or in that place near the foot, if it's particularly strong that thing,
mais toutevoie il covient que tu enquieres celle corrosion, coment elle t’apert;	but still it must be that you inquire about this corrosion, how it has affected you;
et la mundifie en toutes les manieres que tu pues, mais que li voine ou li nerf ne te faicent contraire;	And clean it in all ways you can, but not if it harms your vein or nerve.
et saiches que li incisoire et les soies por coper ces os sont maintes, selonc l’assise des os et l’aparance d’ous,	And know that the saw and chisel are numerous, according to the setting of bones and their appearance,
et lor grossece et lor subtiliteit, et lor grandor et lor petitece, et lor duresce;	and their size and their fineness, and their grandness and their smallness, and their hardness;
et por ceu covient il apareillier a chescune semblance d’ovraige son estrument;	and for that reason it must be equipped with each kind of tool suited to the work of its craft;
